# FlowDesk Progress Snapshot

## Purpose and Update Rule

This is the compact canonical dashboard for FlowDesk roadmap status. It is not a substitute for tests, conformance evidence, durable session evidence, or release approval.

Update this file whenever code, tests, docs, packaging, installer behavior, conformance evidence, release gates, blockers, or user-facing readiness changes. If a work session changes only historical detail, append or correct the relevant archive entry rather than expanding this dashboard. Historical archive files must not be silently rewritten; if a claim is superseded, add a dated correction note.

If no progress fields changed during a non-trivial work session, the final response should state that this snapshot was checked and did not need an update.

- **DEX-2 public API recovery via AWS config only (2026-07-02)**: Production ALB/TG ņäżņĀĢņØä Nginx(80) ĻĖ░ņżĆņ£╝ļĪ£ ļ│ĄĻĄ¼Ē¢łļŗż. `dex-2-sc-vc-api-tg`ņØś active registrationļź╝ `i-0487430b1ea40ee78:80`ņ£╝ļĪ£ ņś«ĻĖ░Ļ│Ā health checkļź╝ `HTTP /api/v1/health-check/` + `HealthCheckPort=80`ņ£╝ļĪ£ ļ¦×ņČś ļÆż, instance SG `DEX-2-SC-VC-API-SG`ņŚÉ ALB SG `ALB-Web-Service-SG` -> tcp/80 ingressļź╝ ņČöĻ░ĆĒ¢łļŗż. Result: `https://dex-2-sc-api.bagel-labs.com/api/v1/health-check/` now returns `HTTP 200` with `{"status":"healthy","database":"ok","cache":"ok"}` and target health is `healthy` on port 80. Note: ELBv2 `describe-target-groups` still reports the target group `Port` metadata as `8004`; the functional traffic path is now `80` and the listener remains unchanged on `443`.

- **Wake notification and capture finalization fix plan (2026-06-24)**: Created `docs/WAKE_AND_CAPTURE_FIX_PLAN_20260624.md` to capture two high-priority reliability blockers and their sequential implementation roadmap. **Problem A**: Capture/finalization convergence failures where lanes produce `safe_capture_ready` session-finalization evidence but fail to materialize terminal `task_result`/`task_failed` records, leaving them `inconsistent_finalizing_without_terminal` indefinitely. Root cause candidate: awaiting-body rescue path in `stall-recovery.ts` contains bare `continue` statements after `safe_capture_ready` detection. **Problem B**: Wake notification loss where inbox rows can be marked `consumed=true` before user sees the notification, and later notices can overwrite earlier ones in the persisted file. Design approach: status/sidebar-first inbox with additive schema fields and best-effort nudge prompts instead of request-response semantics. **Sequential implementation order**: (1) Capture convergence fix with terminal-evidence materialization guard and focused regression tests; (2) Wake notification status-first inbox with additive fields, file-lock safety, and nudge-only prompt refactor. **Authority boundary**: No dispatch, provider selection, fallback/reselection, write/apply, hard-chat/noReply, or Guard authority changes; documentation-only plan pending sequential implementation lanes. **Terminology correction**: Use "current verified authority boundary" instead of "Release 1" for decision labeling to clarify authority/conformance ties. Authority note: docs-only plan capture; no production code, dispatch approval, provider selection, fallback/reselection, write/apply, hard-chat/noReply, or Guard authority changed.
	- Omnigent selection integration design track (2026-06-26): Added `docs/adr/0002-omnigent-selection-integration.md` to authorize Omnigent as a parallel experimental integration track without changing OpenCode Release 1 authority. Added `docs/omnigent/OMNIGENT_DEVELOPMENT_DESIGN_OPTIONS.md` with multiple development approaches (local function MVP, TypeScript CLI bridge, MCP server, Omnigent core PR, OpenCode bridge), selected the local function tool as the first advisory-only path, and explicitly deferred Gemini `antigravity-native` from MVP because OAuth refresh is interactive/TUI-bound. Ran three read-only subtask reviews (architecture, security/policy, verification); all returned `approve_with_changes`. Updated the design to fix schema/role naming drift, add canonical `flowdesk.omnigent_selection.v1` role/response shape, require enum `reason_codes`, replace fallback/retry booleans with `authority="advisory_selection_only"`, use Omnigent transcript/tool-call history as Phase 1 selection evidence instead of a separate required JSONL sidecar, define Phase 1b selection-consistency guard before any dispatch-gate claim, and set `packages/omnigent-tool` as the Python package boundary. Updated Omnigent setup/docs to reflect the installed local environment and correct the future `uv add` path away from the TypeScript `packages/core`. Authority note: docs/ADR/design only; no production code, Omnigent dispatch gate, provider/model fallback, runtime retry, write/apply, hard-chat/noReply, or OpenCode Release 1 authority changed.
		- Omnigent selection Phase 1 minimal implementation (2026-06-26): Added `packages/omnigent-tool` as a standalone Python package exposing `flowdesk_omnigent.selection.select_agent_model` and `flowdesk_select_agent_model`. The selector implements the advisory `flowdesk.omnigent_selection.v1` response, canonical roles, static Claude/GPT registry, Gemini default `non_dispatchable`, enum `reason_codes`, `authority="advisory_selection_only"`, model-family/harness compatibility checks, and optional explicit debug logging only when requested by the caller. Added `examples/omnigent-flowdesk/` orchestrator and four agent fixtures for policy/security, architecture, implementation, and verification. Verification: `PYTHONPATH=packages/omnigent-tool/src /Users/bagel_macpro_055/Documents/work/projects/omnigent/.venv/bin/python -m unittest discover -s packages/omnigent-tool/tests` passed; grep checks found no `sys_session_send`/`sys_session_create`/`sys_read_inbox` or credential-token path/env strings in `packages/omnigent-tool/**/*.py`. Authority note unchanged: advisory selection package and examples only; no Omnigent dispatch gate, provider/model fallback, runtime retry, write/apply, hard-chat/noReply, credential handling, or OpenCode Release 1 authority changed.
			- Omnigent selection live smoke (2026-06-26): Ran real Omnigent `examples/omnigent-flowdesk` smoke against Claude/Codex subscription harnesses. First run proved the three sub-agents could dispatch in parallel and return the sentinel, but `flowdesk_select_agent_model` was not registered because the fixture used an invalid inline top-level tool shape. Added `examples/omnigent-flowdesk/tools/python/flowdesk_select_agent_model.py` as an Omnigent `@tool` wrapper and installed `flowdesk-omnigent-tool` editable into the Omnigent venv with `uv pip install --python /Users/bagel_macpro_055/Documents/work/projects/omnigent/.venv/bin/python -e packages/omnigent-tool`. Second run proved the selection tool registered and returned three `selected` results, but first dispatch failed because the static registry used unavailable model overrides (`anthropic/claude-opus-4-7`, `openai/gpt-5.5`, `openai/gpt-5.4-mini`) for this Omnigent subscription deployment. Updated the registry to use `claude-opus-4-8` for Claude and `model=null` for Codex subscription harness defaults; expanded tests to 8 passing cases. Final first-pass smoke `FLOWDESK_SELECTION_SMOKE_20260626_RETRY` passed: `policy_security`, `architecture`, and `verification` selections all returned `selected` with `authority="advisory_selection_only"`; dispatch used `claude-opus-4-8` for policy/security and omitted model overrides for Codex tasks; all three sub-agents returned `FLOWDESK_OMNIGENT_SELECTION_SMOKE_20260626_RETRY_OK` via inbox. Evidence correction: separate JSONL sidecar evidence is not required for Phase 1; the Omnigent transcript/tool-call history is the source of truth, and Phase 1b should verify selection/dispatch consistency from that history or guardrail context. Authority note unchanged: advisory selection and smoke only; no mechanical Omnigent dispatch gate, fallback/reselection, runtime retry, write/apply, hard-chat/noReply, credential handling, or OpenCode Release 1 authority changed.
				- Omnigent Phase 1b pure trace verifier (2026-06-26): Added `packages/omnigent-tool/src/flowdesk_omnigent/trace_verifier.py` exposing `verify_selection_dispatch_trace(events)` and exported it from `flowdesk_omnigent.__init__`. The verifier consumes normalized `selection`/`dispatch` events and returns `flowdesk.omnigent_trace_verification.v1` with `authority="verification_only"`; it fails dispatches without prior selection, agent mismatch, model mismatch, model override when the selected model is `null`, and dispatch after `blocked`/`non_dispatchable` selection. Added `packages/omnigent-tool/tests/test_trace_verifier.py` with positive and negative consistency cases. Updated Omnigent design docs and package README to distinguish the implemented post-run verifier from a future transcript adapter or mechanical guardrail. Verification: `PYTHONPATH=packages/omnigent-tool/src /Users/bagel_macpro_055/Documents/work/projects/omnigent/.venv/bin/python -m unittest discover -s packages/omnigent-tool/tests` passed with **16 tests OK**. 						- Omnigent Phase 1b trace adapter implementation (2026-06-26): Added `packages/omnigent-tool/src/flowdesk_omnigent/trace_adapter.py` exposing `normalize_omnigent_trace_events(items)` and exported it from `flowdesk_omnigent.__init__`. The adapter consumes Omnigent-like `function_call` / `function_call_output` records plus generic `tool_calls` records, extracts FlowDesk selection outputs and `sys_session_send` dispatch args into redaction-safe normalized trace events, and reports extraction warnings separately from verifier failures. It preserves only fields needed by the verifier (`type`, `task_id`, `selection_id`, `selection_status`, `agent`, `harness`, `model`, `source_ref`) and does not persist raw prompts, full tool args/output, provider payloads, or credentials. Added `packages/omnigent-tool/tests/test_trace_adapter.py` covering three matching selection/dispatch pairs, matching history normalization, nested data shape, blocked-selection dispatch failure, and Codex `model=null` override failure through the verifier. Updated the package README, Omnigent design status table, and Phase backlog checklist. Verification: `PYTHONPATH=packages/omnigent-tool/src /Users/bagel_macpro_055/Documents/work/projects/omnigent/.venv/bin/python -m unittest discover -s packages/omnigent-tool/tests` passed with **21 tests OK**. Authority note unchanged: trace normalization/post-run verification only; no Omnigent dispatch deny gate, provider/model fallback, runtime retry, write/apply, hard-chat/noReply, credential handling, MCP service, upstream hook, or OpenCode Release 1 authority changed.
							- Omnigent Phase 2-4 implementation pass (2026-06-26): Implemented the Phase 2 TypeScript selection CLI bridge in `packages/core/src/omnigent-selection.ts` and `packages/core/src/omnigent-selection-cli.ts`, exported it through `@flowdesk/core`, and added `packages/core/src/omnigent-selection.test.ts`. The CLI reads stdin JSON and emits `flowdesk.omnigent_selection.v1` with `authority="advisory_selection_only"`; Codex subscription selections preserve `model=null`. Updated the Python selector so explicit `engine="ts_cli"` invokes the built Node CLI with a stripped subprocess environment and fails closed without static fallback on CLI failure. Implemented Phase 3 core schema alignment by adding `packages/core/src/omnigent-trace-verification.ts`, validator tests, and `schema-registry.ts` / `schema-artifacts.ts` entries for `flowdesk.omnigent_selection.v1` and `flowdesk.omnigent_trace_verification.v1` as later-release artifacts. Implemented an experimental Phase 4 stdio MCP selection-only server in `packages/omnigent-tool/src/flowdesk_omnigent/mcp_server.py` with console script `flowdesk-omnigent-mcp`; it supports `initialize`, `tools/list`, and `tools/call` for `flowdesk_select_agent_model` only. 													- Omnigent provider-usage snapshot injection (2026-06-30): Extended the Python Omnigent selector so when a request omits both `provider_usage` and `provider_health`, it can load a sanitized usage snapshot from `FLOWDESK_OMNIGENT_PROVIDER_USAGE_JSON` or `FLOWDESK_OMNIGENT_PROVIDER_USAGE_PATH` before applying existing provider availability filtering. Explicit request fields still win over environment/default snapshots, inline JSON wins over file path, snapshot size is bounded, and snapshots containing token/secret/credential-shaped keys are ignored fail-open without echoing raw payloads. Updated the package README with the environment variable contract. - **OMO lane completion reference captured (2026-06-19)**: Expanded `docs/LANE_TERMINATION_REDESIGN.md` with the concrete OMO completion-gate reference so future FlowDesk capture/finalization work does not need to re-search `oh-my-openagent`. The note records that OMO treats `turncompleted`/`step-finish` as activity signals only, completes via `session.idle`/polling after minimum idle deferral, validates assistant/tool output, checks incomplete todos, re-checks the task is still running after async validation, skips active statuses (`busy`/`retry`/`running`), and treats stale/session-gone handling as safety nets. - **P7-S08: routing-advisory-pipeline.ts ŌĆö stale/malformed snapshot fail-closed gate** (2026-06-11): Added `filterValidLedgerEntries` fail-closed gate to `packages/opencode-plugin/src/routing-advisory-pipeline.ts` and extended `RoutingAdvisoryPipelineResultV1` with additive `excludedEntryCount?` and `excludedReasons?` fields. (1) **`filterValidLedgerEntries(entries, options?)`** ŌĆö exported pure function that inspects each `FlowDeskRoutingAdvisoryLedgerEntryV1` and excludes any entry that fails ANY of 4 conditions: (a) `schema_validation_failed` ŌĆö required fields (`signature_ref`, `model_ref`, `weighted_score`, `recorded_at`) missing or wrong type; (b) `score_out_of_range` ŌĆö `weighted_score ├Ś 100` outside 0..100 (catches entries that pass the JSONL loader's structural check but have semantically invalid scores like 1.5 ŌåÆ 150); (c) `schema_hash_mismatch` ŌĆö entry carries a `schema_hash` field that doesn't match `options.schemaHash` when provided; (d) `forbidden_payload_detected` ŌĆö `validateNoForbiddenRawPayloads` returns errors. Returns `{ valid: FlowDeskRoutingAdvisoryLedgerEntryV1[]; excluded: Array<{ reason: string; index: number }> }`. (2) **Pipeline integration** ŌĆö `evaluateAndRecordRoutingAdvisoryV1` now calls `filterValidLedgerEntries(rawEntries)` after loading the ledger. Only `filterResult.valid` entries proceed to signature filtering and gate evaluation. Since `hasEnoughSamples` uses `valid` entry counts, all-excluded ŌåÆ 0 samples < `minSampleCount` ŌåÆ forced `recompute` (fail-closed). `excludedEntryCount` and deduplicated `excludedReasons` are included in the result when non-zero (additive only). (3) **`RoutingAdvisoryPipelineResultV1`** extended with `excludedEntryCount?: number` and `excludedReasons?: string[]`. (4) **Tests** ŌĆö 3 new tests in `packages/opencode-plugin/src/routing-advisory-pipeline.test.ts` under `filterValidLedgerEntries (P7-S08 fail-closed gate)` describe block: S08-1 (malformed entry excluded at unit level + pipeline integration via out-of-range score_out_of_range), S08-2 (schema_hash_mismatch exclusion with matching/missing hash entries), S08-3 (all 3 out-of-range-score entries excluded ŌåÆ pipeline forces recompute fail-closed). All 9 existing tests continue to pass (no regressions). Verification: `npm run typecheck` clean for target files (0 new errors; pre-existing errors in `operational-intelligence.test.ts` and `score-ledger-github-publisher.ts` are pre-existing); `node --test dist/routing-advisory-pipeline.test.js` ŌåÆ **14/14 pass, 0 fail**; full opencode-plugin functional suite ŌåÆ **385/385 pass, 0 fail**.

- **P7-S06: FlowDeskFanoutCadenceDecisionV1 ŌĆö cadence control contract** (2026-06-11): Implemented `packages/core/src/operational-intelligence/multi-model-fanout-cadence.ts` (new file, additive). (1) Defined `FlowDeskFanoutCadenceGateInputV1` input type mirroring `createFlowDeskFanoutCadenceGateV1` parameters plus optional `noveltyScore`, `noveltyThreshold`, `estimatedCostUnits`, `budgetCapUnits`. (2) Defined `FlowDeskFanoutCadenceDecisionOutcomeV1` union type (`allow | blocked_cooldown | blocked_window_cap | blocked_low_novelty | blocked_budget`) ŌĆö named `ŌĆ”OutcomeV1` (not `ŌĆ”LabelV1`) to avoid collision with the identically-named gate-internal type already exported from `gates.ts`. (3) Defined `FlowDeskFanoutCadenceDecisionV1` interface wrapping the gate result with rolling-window, cooldown, novelty, and budget detail fields; authority flags `advisory_only: true`, `dispatch_authority_enabled: false`, `provider_call_authority_enabled: false` are permanently false. (4) Implemented `evaluateFanoutCadenceDecisionV1({ gateInput, now? })` ŌĆö calls `createFlowDeskFanoutCadenceGateV1` internally; on validation failure returns `blocked_window_cap` (fail-closed); precedence order: cooldown ŌåÆ window_cap ŌåÆ low_novelty ŌåÆ budget ŌåÆ allow. (5) Re-exported all three public symbols from `packages/core/src/operational-intelligence/index.ts`. (6) Added `packages/core/src/multi-model-fanout-cadence.test.ts` with 17 tests: allow baseline, blocked_cooldown (with `cooldown_remaining_seconds` value assertion), blocked_window_cap, blocked_low_novelty, blocked_budget, authority flags on all 5 decisions (5 tests), gate validation error fallback, novelty+budget pass-through on allow, cooldown_remaining absent on allow, schema_version constant across all variants, precedence tests (cooldown > window_cap, window_cap > low_novelty), rolling-window field reflection. Verification: `npm run typecheck` clean (0 errors); `node --test dist/multi-model-fanout-cadence.test.js` ŌåÆ 17/17 pass, 0 fail. gates.ts NOT modified (additive principle enforced).



- **P7-S01: FlowDeskScoringEngineInputV1 ĒÖĢņ×ź ŌĆö blockScoring / variantId / proposalSetContext** (2026-06-11): Implemented additive optional field extensions to the scoring engine input interface in `packages/core/src/operational-intelligence/scoring-engine.ts`. Changes: (1) Added three new optional fields to `FlowDeskScoringEngineInputV1`: `blockScoring?: FlowDeskTaskBlockScoringV1` (for judgment 1 real calculation), `variantId?: "simple" | "standard" | "detailed" | "high_assurance"` (variant for detail_fit/simplicity_fit weighting), and `proposalSetContext?: { distinctProviderFamilyCount?: number }` (for model_diversity calculation). (2) Updated `countAvailableInputs()` helper to count the three new optional fields, enabling confidence scoring adjustment when blockScoring is provided. (3) Added validation logic in `scoreWorkflowProposal()`: `blockScoring` is validated via `validateFlowDeskTaskBlockScoringV1()`, and invalid blockScoring does not crash (errors pushed to errors array); `variantId` is validated against allowed values; `proposalSetContext.distinctProviderFamilyCount` is validated as non-negative integer. (4) Implemented variant-based weighting for detail_fit and simplicity_fit dimensions: `detailed` / `high_assurance` ŌåÆ detail_fit weight 1.5, simplicity_fit weight 0.7; `simple` ŌåÆ detail_fit weight 0.7, simplicity_fit weight 1.5; `standard` (default) ŌåÆ both weight 1.0. (5) Implemented model_diversity score calculation from provider family count: 1 family ŌåÆ 50, 2+ families ŌåÆ 85-95 (scaled). (6) Updated dimension score aggregation to use weighted average: `baseAdvisoryScore = sum(score * weight) / sum(weight)` instead of unweighted. All existing callers are unaffected (all new fields are optional, preserved behavior when absent). (7) Added 4 new unit tests in `packages/core/src/operational-intelligence.test.ts`: ŌæĀ blockScoring absent (baseline score 68), ŌæĪ blockScoring present (confidence increases to 60, advisory score 70), Ōæó variantId weight effects (detailed > simple due to detail_fit weighting), ŌæŻ proposalSetContext distinctProviderFamilyCount effects (higher diversity score for multi-provider). Verification: `npm run typecheck` clean (pre-existing unrelated type errors in index.ts untouched); test runs show 4 new tests pass (plus 1173 existing tests in core package). No regressions in existing behavior.

(1) **Types**: `FlowDeskScoreLedgerPartitionStateV1` (union of "raw" | "sealed" | "immutable"), `FlowDeskScoreLedgerPartitionV1` (partition metadata with state transitions, hashes, sealing windows, grace periods, advisory-only authority flags), `FlowDeskScoreLedgerManifestV1` (manifest container for partition array + optional trusted chain head), `FlowDeskTrustedChainHeadV1` (immutable anchor record). (3) **Creators**: `createFlowDeskScoreLedgerPartitionV1()` with state-transition pre-validation; `createFlowDeskScoreLedgerManifestV1()` builds manifest from partitions; `createFlowDeskTrustedChainHeadV1()` builds immutable anchor.
